        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function shouldLoadOneTrustScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithOneTrustEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithOneTrustEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithOneTrustEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            script.setAttribute("data-domain-script", DATA_DOMAIN_SCRIPT);

            return script;
        }

        function loadCCPAAddon() {
            loadScript(CCPA_ADDON.url, "text/javascript", CCPA_ADDON.options);
        }

        function preloadBannerSdk() {
            const link = document.createElement("link");
            link.href = BANNER_SDK.url;
            link.rel = "preload";
            link.as = "script";

            document.head.appendChild(link);
        }

        function oneTrustLoaded() {
            return !!(window.OneTrust || window.OneTrustStub);
        }

        console.debug('OneTrust setup', countriesWithOneTrustEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !oneTrustLoaded()) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!oneTrustLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadOneTrustScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (function () {
        function shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            const countriesWithKetchEnabled = {"countries":["IN","HU","SG"]};
            if (!countriesWithKetchEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithKetchEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }
            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithKetchEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }


        function loadKetchScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            if (!shouldLoadKetchScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region)) {
                return;
            }

            window.semaphore = window.semaphore || [];

            window.ketch = function () {
                window.semaphore.push(arguments);
            };

            var urlParams = new URLSearchParams(document.location.search);
            var property = urlParams.has("property") ? urlParams.get("property") : "website_smart_tag";

            var scriptElement = document.createElement("script");
            scriptElement.type = "text/javascript";
            scriptElement.src = "https://global.ketchcdn.com/web/v2/config/fandom/" + property + "/boot.js";
            scriptElement.defer = scriptElement.async = true;

            document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(scriptElement);
        }

        function ketchLoaded() {
            return !!window.ketch;
        }

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        async function waitForGeoAndLoadScripts() {
            const geo = await waitForGeo();
            if (geo && !ketchLoaded()) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            }
        }

        if (!ketchLoaded()) {
            const geo = getGeo();

            if (geo) {
                loadKetchScripts(geo);
            } else {
                waitForGeoAndLoadScripts();
            }
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
    (async function () {
        // const AIRGAP_URL = '<script
        // data-cfasync="false"
        // src=""
        const AIRGAP_URL = 'https://transcend-cdn.com/cm/54b0c313-5d22-47e5-92fd-f979a37d1ad0/airgap.js';
        const countriesWithAirgapEnabled = [];

        function getCookieValue(cookieName) {

            const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
            return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
        }

        function getGeo() {
            try {
                return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo')));
            } catch {
                return null;
            }
        }

        function loadAirgapScripts(geo) {
            const country = geo.country.toUpperCase();
            const region = geo.region.toUpperCase();
            const enabled = shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) || airgapScriptForced();

            if (!enabled) {
                return;
            }

            loadScript(AIRGAP_URL, "text/javascript", {
                'data-cfasync': false
            });
        }

        // VARIABLE EXAMPLE
        // countriesWithAirgapEnabled = {
        //     "countries": ["TR","PL"],
        //     "regions": ["CA","NY"]
        // }

        function airgapScriptForced() {
            return window.location.search.includes('icPreferredCMP=airgap');
        }

        function shouldLoadAirgapScriptsBasedOnWikiConfigVariable(country, region) {
            if (!countriesWithAirgapEnabled || Object.keys(countriesWithAirgapEnabled).length === 0) {
                return false;
            }

            if (country === 'US') {
                const regionsToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.regions;

                if (Array.isArray(regionsToLoad) && regionsToLoad.length > 0) {
                    if (regionsToLoad.includes(region)) {
                        return true;
                    }
                }
            }

            const countriesToLoad = countriesWithAirgapEnabled.countries;

            if (Array.isArray(countriesToLoad) && countriesToLoad.length > 0) {
                return countriesToLoad.includes(country);
            }
        }

        function loadScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = createScript(url, type, options);

            document.head.appendChild(script);
        }

        function createScript(url, type, options) {
            const script = document.createElement("script");

            script.src = url;
            script.type = type;
            script.async = true;

            for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(options)) {
                script.setAttribute(key, value);
            }

            return script;
        }

        console.debug('Airgap setup', countriesWithAirgapEnabled);

        function waitForGeo() {
            return new Promise((resolve) => {
                let counter = 0;
                const maxCount = 10;
                const interval = setInterval(() => {
                    const geo = getGeo();
                    if (geo || counter >= maxCount) {
                        clearInterval(interval);
                        resolve(geo);
                    }
                    counter++;
                }, 100);
            });
        }

        let geo = getGeo();

        if (geo === null) {
            geo = await waitForGeo();
        }

        if (geo) {
            loadAirgapScripts(geo);
        }
    })();
</script>

<script>
	const useMaxDefaultContentWidth = Boolean(false);

	const defaultContentWidth = useMaxDefaultContentWidth ? 'expanded' : 'collapsed';

	let contentWidthPreference;

	try {
		contentWidthPreference = localStorage.getItem('contentwidth') || defaultContentWidth;
	} catch (e) {
		contentWidthPreference = defaultContentWidth;
	}

	if ( contentWidthPreference === 'expanded' ) {
		document.documentElement.classList.add('is-content-expanded');
	}
</script>

													<script data-name="featured-video-mapped-to-wiki">
	(function () {
		// we can't use mw.config here because it's too early so we need to pass this data in different way
		const videoDetails = {
			mapping: {"mediaId":"sXWp3rZ0","connatixPlaylistId":"36081eca-e784-4e30-87c3-133cf673e447","impressionsPerSession":4},
			impressionsPerSession: 4,
		};
		const videoBridgeCountries = ["AE","AG","AL","AM","AR","AT","AU","AZ","BA","BB","BD","BG","BH","BN","BO","BR","BS","BY","CA","CH","CL","CN","CO","CR","CU","CY","CZ","DE","DK","DO","DZ","EC","EE","EG","ES","FI","FR","GB","GE","GF","GG","GH","GP","GR","GT","GU","GY","HK","HN","HR","HU","ID","IE","IL","IM","IN","IQ","IR","IS","IT","JE","JM","JO","JP","KE","KG","KH","KR","KW","KY","KZ","LA","LB","LK","LT","LU","LV","LY","MA","MD","ME","MK","MM","MN","MO","MQ","MT","MU","MV","MX","MY","NG","NI","NO","NP","NZ","OM","PA","PE","PH","PK","PL","PR","PS","PT","PY","QA","RE","RO","RS","RU","SA","SC","SE","SG","SI","SK","SV","TD","TH","TN","TR","TT","TW","UA","US","UY","UZ","VE","VI","VN","ZA","ZW"];
		const tier3VideoBridgeCountries = ["GB","BE","NL","DE","AU","MX","AR","FR","MD","CA","ES","IT","PE","CO","CL","NZ"];
		let hasVideoOnPage = null;

		function getCookieValue(cookieName) {
			const cookieSplit = ('; ' + document.cookie).split('; ' + cookieName + '=');
			return cookieSplit.length === 2 ? cookieSplit.pop().split(';').shift() : null;
		}

		function hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki() {
			const impressionsSoFar = Number(getCookieValue('playerImpressionsInWiki')) || 0;
			const allowedImpressions = Number(videoDetails.impressionsPerSession);

			return impressionsSoFar >= allowedImpressions;
		}

		function getCountryCode() {
			try {
				return JSON.parse(decodeURIComponent(getCookieValue('Geo'))).country.toLowerCase();
			} catch {
				return null;
			}
		}

		function isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() {
			const countryCode = getCountryCode();

			if (!countryCode) {
				return false;
			}

			// If it's a default mapping, then check the country whitelist from the default mapping.
			if (videoDetails?.mapping?.isDefaultMapping) {
				// If the wiki is classified as a tier3 wiki, then check the country whitelist from the tier3VideoBridge whitelist.
				const allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis = tier3VideoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedTier3CountryCode) {
					return allowedTier3CountryCode.toLowerCase();
				})

				return allowedCountriesForTier3Wikis.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			} else {
				// If not a default mapping wiki (so it's a wiki mapping), then check the country whitelist from the videoBridge whitelist
				const allowedCountries = videoBridgeCountries.map(function (allowedCountryCode) {
					return allowedCountryCode.toLowerCase();
				});

				return allowedCountries.indexOf(countryCode) !== -1;
			}
		}

		window.fandomIsVideoPossible = function () {
			if (hasVideoOnPage === null) {
				hasVideoOnPage =
					videoDetails.mapping &&
					isVideoBridgeAllowedForCountry() &&
					!hasMaxedOutPlayerImpressionsInWiki();
			}

			return hasVideoOnPage;
		};

		window.canPlayVideo = function () {
			return window.fandomIsVideoPossible()
		};

		if (!window.canPlayVideo()) {
			document.body.classList.add('no-featured-video');
		} else {
			document.body.classList.add('has-featured-video');
		}
	})();
</script>

</p><p>The <b>Going Merry</b><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> was the first full-sized <a href="/wiki/Ship" title="Ship">ship</a> owned by the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a>, a <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/caravel" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:caravel">caravel</a> that served as their main transportation through the <a href="/wiki/East_Blue" title="East Blue">East Blue</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> up until <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>. It was often affectionally referred to as simply <b>Merry</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">メリー</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Merī</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span> by the crew.
</p><p>Originally designed by <a href="/wiki/Kaya" title="Kaya">Kaya</a>'s servant <a href="/wiki/Merry" title="Merry">Merry</a>, it was gifted to the Straw Hats for defending <a href="/wiki/Syrup_Village" title="Syrup Village">Syrup Village</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Black_Cat_Pirates" title="Black Cat Pirates">Black Cat Pirates</a>. Over time, it came to be loved by the crew as a home and as a friend, so much so that she eventually developed a life of her own and became a genuine crew member. Unfortunately, the Going Merry took an inordinate amount of damage during her "lifetime", being blown up, impaled, sliced up multiple times, and partially <a href="/wiki/Baku_Baku_no_Mi" title="Baku Baku no Mi">eaten</a> by <a href="/wiki/Wapol" title="Wapol">Wapol</a>. Eventually, the Merry could no longer continue and after helping the Straw Hats escape <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>, it received a Viking funeral.<sup id="cite_ref-c430_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c430-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After destruction, the Merry was succeeded by the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, a ship specially built by <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a> (and the <a href="/wiki/Galley-La_Company" title="Galley-La Company">Galley-La Company</a>) to maintain the "soul" of its predecessor.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Ship_Design_and_Appearance">Ship Design and Appearance</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D1&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The Going Merry was a medium-sized caravel with a sheep theme appearance, with woody brown tones and white wooden details that curled up to simulate sheep's wool. He had a jib and a central steer rudder, but it was considerably smaller and simpler than most ships seen in the series. The Going Merry had two masts, one containing a simple square sail bearing the Straw Hat Pirates' Jolly Roger, with a platform at the top that allowed a wide view of the sea, and the other containing a triangular sail with red and white stripes. Both masts bore flags bearing the Jolly Roger of the crew and several ropes tied to its support that were attached to the deck . The deck contained several barrels containing supplies, a wooden floor and white painted handrails. The anchor is located at the front, near the figurehead and attached to the handrail. At the back was a cabin where the kitchen was located. The ship's armaments consisted of four cannons, one in the bow pointing forward, one in the stern, and two pointing to either side. They were rarely used, as the Straw Hat Pirates usually preferred to run away or engage in hand-to-hand combat. After the Arlong Park Arc, the Going Merry gained three tangerine trees from <a href="/wiki/Bell-m%C3%A8re" title="Bell-mère">Bell-mère</a>'s orchard, a memento of Nami's home. As the crew traveled through the <a href="/wiki/Paradise" title="Paradise">first half</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>, the ship received more and more damage and gained several metal patches to hold her together at places that could not be nailed back together: prominent examples are Merry's figurehead and the mast, which was torn off several times, and its deck, which showed various damages such as loose wooden boards. Several spots of the guardrail were damaged and missing, leading the crew to patch them up with wood-boards, which was done rather crudely due to their lack of experience in carpentry. By the time it reached <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>, the keel was damaged, which was considered to be irreparable in the long run, thus dooming Merry. In the Skypiea arc, the body of the ship had wings and the sheep figurehead was dressed as a chicken. 
</p><p>Despite the incredible amount of damage the ship accumulated over its travel through the Grand Line, it had a miraculous resilience in that when Kaku released it to drop down a waterfall, it did not smash apart, but instead landed on its side, undamaged from the fall. With Iceburg's expertise in patching it up to extend the limited time it had, the Going Merry was able to sail through the treacherous storm of the <a href="/wiki/Aqua_Laguna" title="Aqua Laguna">Aqua Laguna</a>, all the way to <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a> and back before finally succumbing to its limits. Despite this, Merry was an extremely obsolete project even before the events of East Blue, and according to the Galley-la boatswains, it was dangerous for the Straw Hats to continue sailing on her due to it being a caravel, a class of ships that was considered unsuitable for this type of adventures despite its high mobility.
</p><p>In <a href="/wiki/Volume_11" title="Volume 11">Volume 11</a> of the manga, <a href="/wiki/Eiichiro_Oda" title="Eiichiro Oda">Oda</a> presented various schematics and explanations of each part of the ship. These included everything from Merry's figurehead to the kitchen.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div style="text-align: center; font-size: 0.7em; color: ; margin: 0.7em 0;"><span style="display: inline-block; vertical-align: top; width: 172px; margin-right: 10px; margin-bottom: 10px;"><table style="width: 172px; height: 172px; border: 1px solid #3366CC; padding: 10px; border-spacing: 0;"><tbody><tr><td style="text-align: center; vertical-align: middle; padding: 0px;"><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Going_Merry_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest?cb=20211106081621" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry Digitally Colored Manga" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/ba/Going_Merry_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20211106081621" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="136" data-image-name="Going Merry Digitally Colored Manga.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry_Digitally_Colored_Manga.png" data-relevant="1" /></a></td></tr></tbody></table><div style="text-align: center;">The Going Merry in the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>.

<h3><span id="Meeting_Room.2C_Lounge.2C_and_Helm"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Meeting_Room,_Lounge,_and_Helm">Meeting Room, Lounge, and Helm</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D2&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/32/Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721205736" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Lounge Layout" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="240" height="168" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Lounge Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/32/Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240721205736" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/32/Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721205736" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Lounge Layout" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/32/Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240721205736" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="240" height="168" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Lounge Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/32/Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/240?cb=20240721205736" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Lounge_Layout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Meeting room, Lounge, and Helm of the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>This is the room with the most functions in the entire ship. It serves as the meeting room, lounge, kitchen and helm. Here the whole crew can do a number of things. Temporarily, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> used this room for his <b>Usopp's Workshop</b>.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Unlike other pirate ships, the Going Merry did not have a rudder, and its steering was controlled by a steering pole located in this room. It has a sheep's head similar to the one used for the ship's figurehead. By tilting the pole left or right, the rudder at the stern will move in that direction.
</p>
<h3><span id="Men.27s_Room"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Men's_Room">Men's Room</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D3&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721205934" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Men&#39;s Room Layout" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Men&#39;s Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721205934" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721205934" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Men&#39;s Room Layout" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721205934" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Men&#39;s Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721205934" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Men%27s_Room_Layout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Men's room of the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The men's room of the Going Merry is located below the deck of the ship right below the mast. It is quite large and untidy. This room is normally crowded due to the fact it is shared by <a href="/wiki/Monkey_D._Luffy" title="Monkey D. Luffy">Luffy</a>, <a href="/wiki/Roronoa_Zoro" title="Roronoa Zoro">Zoro</a>, <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a>, <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Sanji" title="Sanji">Sanji</a> to sleep. It is accessed through a hatch next to the mast. There are a total of five hammocks located here to sleep on. There is an emergency exit that connects to the women's room in case something should happen. It has a laundry set in the corner and each guy responsible for their own laundry. <br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span id="Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_.28aft.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_(aft)">Storage Room and Cannon Deck (aft)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D4&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721210616" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Storage Room and Cannon Deck Room Layout" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Storage Room and Cannon Deck Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210616" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721210616" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Storage Room and Cannon Deck Room Layout" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210616" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Storage Room and Cannon Deck Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/3/30/Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210616" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Storage_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Storage room and Cannon deck(aft) of the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>A storage room and a cannon deck are located under the lounge of the Going Merry. This is where the crew keeps all their cargo such as beer barrels, water barrels, rations, and treasure boxes in storage. Any treasure that Nami cannot keep in the women's quarters is kept here as well. The room also houses two cannons facing each side of the ship.
</p><p>The bathroom and the women's quarters can be accessed from here. Some towels can be found next to the bathroom's entrance for when one finishes taking a bath. The hatch going down to the women's quarters had a latch to keep out prying eyes.
</p><p>The steering shaft that is used to steer the ship can also be seen located above this room.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span id="Women.27s_Room"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Women's_Room">Women's Room</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D5&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721210903" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Women&#39;s Room Layout" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="169" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Women&#39;s Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210903" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721210903" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Women&#39;s Room Layout" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210903" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="169" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Women&#39;s Room Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/2/2f/Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721210903" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Women%27s_Room_Layout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Women's room of the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The women's room of the Going Merry is located under the storage and cannon deck. This is where <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a> (and for a time, <a href="/wiki/Nefertari_Vivi" title="Nefertari Vivi">Vivi</a>) usually sleep. It was originally designed by Merry for Kaya's use, resulting in its beautiful and well-decorated design. The room is accessed through a hatch that leads to the room above. This hatch had a lock. There is an emergency exit that connects to the men's room located here in case something happens. This hatch, however, is not normally used and is usually locked.
</p><p>After the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Park_Arc" title="Arlong Park Arc">Arlong Park Arc</a>, a bar was added here by a carpenter from Cocoyasi, <a href="/wiki/Teru" title="Teru">Teru-san</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span id="Cannon_Deck_.28fore.29_and_Anchor_Room"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Cannon_Deck_(fore)_and_Anchor_Room">Cannon Deck (fore) and Anchor Room</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D6&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 240px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/9/99/Going_Merry%27s_Anchor_Room_and_Cannon_Deck_Room_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721211222" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s <p>A cannon deck can be found below the front deck of the Going Merry. It also serves as the room where the anchor is stored. Various weapons such as swords can be stored here. It also contains giant oars and life preservers for use when called for.
</p><p>The cannon here was notably used to fire at <a href="/wiki/Laboon" title="Laboon">Laboon</a> before the Going Merry rammed into him and broke her figurehead.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Bathroom">Bathroom</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D7&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 250px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721211637" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Bathroom and Water-Drawing Machine Layout" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Bathroom and Water-Drawing Machine Layout.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721211637" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721211637" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Bathroom and Water-Drawing Machine Layout" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721211637" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="250" height="163" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Bathroom and Water-Drawing Machine Layout.png" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/250?cb=20240721211637" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Bathroom_and_Water-Drawing_Machine_Layout.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Bathroom of the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The bathroom of the Going Merry is located below deck, next to the rudder of the ship. It is accessed through a door leading to the storage room. This door had curtains for privacy.
</p><p>The bathroom features a shower, a bathtub, a sink, and a toilet. When <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Robin</a> was frozen by <a href="/wiki/Kuzan" title="Kuzan">Aokiji</a>, the bathtub was used by <a href="/wiki/Tony_Tony_Chopper" title="Tony Tony Chopper">Chopper</a> and <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> to thaw her out.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> The water in the bathroom is drawn up by a special machine located underneath the stairs on the top deck. There used to be two of these machines, but Luffy broke one.
</p><p>Care must be taken after using the shower. After cleaning themselves, the crew must make sure to thoroughly clean the bathroom with a rubber wiper in order to prevent the ship from being weakened by moisture.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h3><span id="Luffy.27s_Favorite_Seat"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Luffy's_Favorite_Seat">Luffy's Favorite Seat</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D8&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721212134" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Headpiece" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="191" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Headpiece.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212134" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721212134" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Headpiece" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212134" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="191" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Headpiece.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/d3/Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212134" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Headpiece.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Luffy's Favorite Seat, the figurehead of the Going  Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>The figurehead of the Going Merry is a sheep. This is where Luffy likes to sit most of the time while sailing. Why he likes to sit there considering his inability to swim is a complete mystery. When the figurehead was temporarily broken upon impact with <a href="/wiki/Laboon" title="Laboon">Laboon</a>, Luffy expressed how mad he was and attacked the whale. The figurehead is also found on top of the ship's steering pole in the main room. This design is also used for the figurehead of the <a href="/wiki/Mini_Merry_II" title="Mini Merry II">Mini Merry II</a>.
</p><p>Throughout the series, the figurehead would sometimes show signs of expressions like a regular person. These have ranged from comical to sad.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="Nami.27s_Mikan_Trees"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Nami's_Mikan_Trees">Nami's Mikan Trees</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D9&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721212358" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Nami&#39;s Orange Fields" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="191" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Nami&#39;s Orange Fields.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212358" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png/revision/latest?cb=20240721212358" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Nami&#39;s Orange Fields" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212358" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="191" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Nami&#39;s Orange Fields.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/f/f1/Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20240721212358" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Nami%27s_Orange_Fields.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Nami's Mikan Trees on the Going Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Park_Arc" title="Arlong Park Arc">Arlong Park Arc</a>, three <a href="/wiki/Foods#Mikan" title="Foods">mikan</a> trees from Bell-mère's grove were added to the top of the Going Merry. The fruits they bear are satsumas (Citrus unshui) but are usually translated as tangerine or oranges. Nami treats them with care, as they are mementos of Bell-mère. They provide the crew with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vitamin_C" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Vitamin C">Vitamin C</a> as well as serve as decorations for the ship.
</p><p>Aside from Nami taking care of them, Sanji also protects these three trees from those who might otherwise harm them or steal the fruit (e.g., Luffy).
</p><p>After Luffy and Usopp's battle in Water 7, these trees were moved to the hotel room where the Straw Hats were. They were luckily found by the <a href="/wiki/Galley-La_Company" title="Galley-La Company">Galley-La</a> <a href="/wiki/Shipwright" title="Shipwright">shipwrights</a> and moved to a safer location before the <a href="/wiki/Aqua_Laguna" title="Aqua Laguna">Aqua Laguna</a> hit.
</p><p>They, along with the rest of the Straw Hats' belongings, now reside on the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="History">History</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D10&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Commissioning">Commissioning</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D11&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>The Going Merry was first conceptualized by <a href="/wiki/Merry" title="Merry">Merry</a> approximately two years after <a href="/wiki/Gol_D._Roger" title="Gol D. Roger">Gold Roger</a>'s execution, roughly contemporaneous with <a href="/wiki/Shiki" title="Shiki">Shiki</a>'s escape from <a href="/wiki/Impel_Down" title="Impel Down">Impel Down</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Eventually, it was completed as a luxury vessel for <a href="/wiki/Kaya" title="Kaya">Kaya</a>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="East_Blue_Saga">East Blue Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D12&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Syrup_Village_Arc">Syrup Village Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D13&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ac/Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png/revision/latest?cb=20121208225800" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Original Appearance" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Original Appearance.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ac/Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20121208225800" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ac/Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png/revision/latest?cb=20121208225800" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Original Appearance" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ac/Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20121208225800" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Original Appearance.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/ac/Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20121208225800" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Original_Appearance.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Going Merry in its original form being presented by Merry.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After successfully defending <a href="/wiki/Syrup_Village" title="Syrup Village">Syrup Village</a> from <a href="/wiki/Kuro" title="Kuro">Captain Kuro</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Black_Cat_Pirates" title="Black Cat Pirates">Black Cat Pirates</a>, Usopp asked that the <a href="/wiki/Straw_Hat_Pirates" title="Straw Hat Pirates">Straw Hat Pirates</a> be given a proper ship (their original reason for visiting). Moved by their heroism, Kaya and Merry agreed to grant the Going Merry, with Merry even personally stocking it and explaining its workings to <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a>. Overjoyed, the Straw Hats wasted no time in boarding it, accepting Usopp as their newest crewmate, and setting off for further adventures.<sup id="cite_ref-c41_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c41-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="One_Piece:_The_Movie">One Piece: The Movie</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D14&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Baratie_Arc">Baratie Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D15&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Sailing on the Merry began quite peacefully, the Straw Hats busying themselves with designing a proper <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a> and testing the cannons. However, one test-shot nearly hit the <a href="/wiki/Bounty_hunter" class="mw-redirect" title="Bounty hunter">bounty hunters</a> <a href="/wiki/Johnny" title="Johnny">Johnny</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yosaku" title="Yosaku">Yosaku</a>, drawing a furious counterattack. Johnny, in a fit of desperation, turned his swords on the crew and chopped off part of the railing on the Merry's upper deck. However, after the Straw Hats treated Yosaku's scurvy with limes from the pantry, the bounty hunters became allies, and inspired their next destination: the sea restaurant <a href="/wiki/Baratie" title="Baratie">Baratie</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During a raid by <a href="/wiki/Krieg" title="Krieg">Don Krieg</a>, which was further complicated by the appearance of <a href="/wiki/Dracule_Mihawk" title="Dracule Mihawk">Dracule Mihawk</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nami" title="Nami">Nami</a> stole the Going Merry and headed back to <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a> and his crew, bringing the ship and the crew's treasures with her.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Arlong_Park_Arc">Arlong Park Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D16&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Alone, Nami sailed the Merry to the <a href="/wiki/Conomi_Islands" title="Conomi Islands">Conomi Islands</a>, anchoring it close to her hometown of <a href="/wiki/Cocoyasi_Village" title="Cocoyasi Village">Cocoyasi Village</a>. It remained there, apparently untouched, until the Straw Hats had defeated the <a href="/wiki/Arlong_Pirates" title="Arlong Pirates">Arlong Pirates</a>.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Episode_Special_1">Episode Special 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D17&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">


<tbody><tr>
<td><span style="font-size:95%"><b>This is an <a href="/wiki/Category:Pages_With_Empty_Sections" title="Category:Pages With Empty Sections"><font color="maroon">empty section</font></a>. Please help the wiki by adding information to it.</b><span>
</span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Loguetown_Arc">Loguetown Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D18&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the battle with <a href="/wiki/Arlong" title="Arlong">Arlong</a>, the Going Merry was later reclaimed and given three mikan trees, which were planted on top of the ship's cabin, where they remained. The Merry then continued on her voyage towards the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a>. While sailing towards their destination, the crew made a stop at the last island in East Blue before entering the Grand Line, <a href="/wiki/Loguetown" title="Loguetown">Loguetown</a>, in order to stock up on supplies for the journey ahead. This stop had something important for everyone. After docking the ship on a shore far from town in order to avoid drawing the attention of the <a href="/wiki/Marines" title="Marines">Marines</a> stationed there, the crew went into town to complete their tasks. This trip, which was already then made complicated by the reappearance of <a href="/wiki/Buggy" title="Buggy">Buggy the Clown</a> and the pursuit of <a href="/wiki/Smoker" title="Smoker">Smoker</a>'s Marines, was abruptly ended with the appearance of a massive storm. This storm stopped the Going Merry from being burnt by <a href="/wiki/Mohji" title="Mohji">Mohji</a> and the Marines, as matches could not be lit, and the Marine's gunpowder supply was wet.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After escaping from Loguetown, the crew then held a small ceremony on board the Going Merry before entering the <a href="/wiki/Grand_Line" title="Grand Line">Grand Line</a> while the storm raged on, symbolized by placing their feet above a barrel. The entire crew vowed to accomplish all of their dreams. With that done, the Going Merry was then <a href="/wiki/Navigator" title="Navigator">navigated</a> towards <a href="/wiki/Reverse_Mountain" title="Reverse Mountain">Reverse Mountain</a>, the entrance to the Grand Line.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Clockwork_Island_Adventure">Clockwork Island Adventure</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D19&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Warship_Island_Arc">Warship Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D20&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arabasta_Saga">Arabasta Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D21&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Reverse_Mountain_Arc">Reverse Mountain Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D22&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the Going Merry traversed Reverse Mountain and entered the Grand Line, the ship immediately encountered an <a href="/wiki/Animal_Species#Island_Whales" title="Animal Species">Island Whale</a> named <a href="/wiki/Laboon" title="Laboon">Laboon</a>. After crashing into the whale's side and knocking the figurehead off, an infuriated Luffy punched the whale in the eye. The whale, angered by this attack, swallowed the entire ship and most of the crew. Luffy was not swallowed along with the rest of the crew and the ship but instead found a trap door on the whale's side and went in.
</p><p>While inside the whale, the crew met <a href="/wiki/Crocus" title="Crocus">Crocus</a>, as well as <a href="/wiki/Mr._9" title="Mr. 9">Mr. 9</a> and <a href="/wiki/Nefertari_Vivi" title="Nefertari Vivi">Miss Wednesday</a>. After they got out of the whale, Luffy broke the mast off the Going Merry and attacked the whale with it. Both the whale and Luffy fought until Luffy called off the fight, announcing that it was a draw. Luffy then told the whale that he would return to Reverse Mountain to finish the fight and that the whale was not allowed to hit his head against the mountain anymore. The mast was reattached with the first of many tin plates that would coat its multiple fractures, and the figurehead was repaired in a similar manner.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Whisky_Peak_Arc">Whisky Peak Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D23&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Nami learned about <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Poses</a> from Crocus, and the crew then escorted Mr. 9 and Miss Wednesday back to their home island, <a href="/wiki/Whisky_Peak" title="Whisky Peak">Whisky Peak</a>, unbeknownst to them that the two were really planning something. After several events on the island where the crew learned about the secret organization, Baroque Works, its doings, and the true identity of Miss Wednesday, the Going Merry was then steered away from Whisky Peak with two extra passengers, Vivi, who disguised herself as Miss Wednesday, and <a href="/wiki/Karoo" title="Karoo">Karoo</a>, Vivi's pet spot billed duck. The Going Merry then sailed in the direction of Little Garden via the Log Pose where the crew experienced more Baroque Works related endeavors.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Little_Garden_Arc">Little Garden Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D24&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Hakoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230322222254" class="image"><img alt="Hakoku" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Hakoku.png" data-image-key="Hakoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Hakoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230322222254" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Hakoku.png/revision/latest?cb=20230322222254" class="image"><img alt="Hakoku" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Hakoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230322222254" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Hakoku.png" data-image-key="Hakoku.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a7/Hakoku.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230322222254" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Hakoku.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Going Merry being propelled through the Island Eater by an attack from Dorry and Brogy.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After surviving the battle brought about by Mr. 3, the Going Merry and its crew left Little Garden and headed in the direction of Arabasta using an Eternal Pose left by the aforementioned villain. They left Little Garden for their journey to Arabasta but not before the ship was temporarily swallowed by an Island Eater, which was shortly blown to bits by Dorry and Brogy. The journey to Vivi's homeland was at first smooth sailing until it was discovered that Nami was sick. This sickness, which no one in the crew could treat, forced the Going Merry and her crew to make a slight detour to the nearest island to find a doctor, <a href="/wiki/Drum_Island" title="Drum Island">Drum Island</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Drum_Island_Arc">Drum Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D25&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After defeating Wapol and his men (during which Wapol had bitten a piece of the ship's side), whose ship they encountered earlier before coming to Drum, the Going Merry acquired a new member to her list of occupants; the reindeer doctor, Chopper. With that, the crew continued on its journey to Arabasta. While journeying to Arabasta, the ship accidentally took on board another passenger due to Luffy and Usopp's fishing techniques and some steam created by an underwater volcano. This person, Mr. 2 Bon Kurei, entertained the crew until his ship and crew came to the Going Merry to fetch him back. Upon learning the identity and powers of this person, the crew and their companions decided to protect themselves using an X mark placed on each of their right forearms and some bandages covering it. With this, they swore aboard the Going Merry as friends.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Arabasta_Arc">Arabasta Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D26&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After reaching Arabasta and docking in Nanohana, the Going Merry briefly took on board another passenger, Luffy's brother, <a href="/wiki/Portgas_D._Ace" title="Portgas D. Ace">Portgas D. Ace</a>. After a short meeting with Ace about <a href="/wiki/Marshall_D._Teach" title="Marshall D. Teach">Blackbeard</a>, the Going Merry was steered to the southwestern shores of Arabasta, across the great river, where it remained for some time. After <a href="/wiki/Crocodile" title="Crocodile">Crocodile</a> was defeated, it was learned that Mr. 2 had taken the ship. Learning about this the crew sped across the vast desert to retrieve their ship. Upon reaching the ship, it was learned that Mr. 2 had taken the ship not as an enemy but as a friend. He had taken the ship in order to safeguard it from the various Marines that were then searching around the island for the Straw Hats. With the crew back on the Going Merry and the Straw Hats' business with Baroque Works finished, it was time to leave Arabasta.
</p><p>Leaving Arabasta was a real obstacle for the Going Merry. Being pursued by the various Marine ships under Captain Hina, the Going Merry suffered heavily from battle damage. The metal poles that were shot from the Marine ships pierced the ship's side thus creating large holes in the Merry's frame. Fortunately, however, the reformed Mr. 2, along with his crew, was able to draw away the Marines then by pretending to be the Straw Hats thus saving the ship from further damage. After all that, the Going Merry was steered to the northeastern part of the Arabasta. Here the Straw Hats were to meet up with Vivi in case she wanted to join up with the crew. Vivi was at the meeting place; however, she declined the offer for the sake of her country. The crew wanted to respond to Vivi from aboard the Merry; however, they could not due to a nearby Marine ship. Not wanting to get Vivi in trouble, the crew instead responded by showing off their X marks to Vivi. With that sign of friendship, the Going Merry and its crew sailed away from Arabasta.
</p><p>The escapades with Baroque Works had left the crew of the Going Merry very tired and lonely due to the fact that Vivi wasn't coming along. However, one last surprise came along from all this: the former vice president of Baroque Works, Miss All Sunday, had stowed away aboard the Going Merry. Having met her before leaving Whisky Peak and identifying her as a past enemy, the crew did not know what to do. The woman, whose real name was <a href="/wiki/Nico_Robin" title="Nico Robin">Nico Robin</a>, surprisingly asked to join the crew due to actions done by Luffy. This, Luffy accepted and the Going Merry gained another occupant from this series of events involving Baroque Works.
</p>
<h4><span id="Chopper.27s_Kingdom_on_the_Island_of_Strange_Animals"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Chopper's_Kingdom_on_the_Island_of_Strange_Animals">Chopper's Kingdom on the Island of Strange Animals</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D27&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Cursed_Holy_Sword">The Cursed Holy Sword</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D34&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Ruluka_Island_Arc">Ruluka Island Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D35&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">
