</span></span></td></tr></tbody></table>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Jaya_Arc">Jaya Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D36&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the events with Baroque Works, the Going Merry and her crew shortly experienced an incredible sight. A ship fell out of the sky. This ship, later identified to be the <a href="/wiki/St._Briss" title="St. Briss">St. Briss</a>, apparently came from a sky island called <a href="/wiki/Skypiea" title="Skypiea">Skypiea</a>. This idea of this island seemed quite impossible. However, it appeared to be the next destination on the <a href="/wiki/Log_Pose" title="Log Pose">Log Pose</a>. With this new sensation, Luffy decided to steer the Going Merry to Skypiea, but there was one slight problem. The Going Merry was not capable of going into the sky. Unable to do anything, the ship was instead steered into the direction of <a href="/wiki/Jaya" title="Jaya">Jaya</a> where the crew hoped to find some answers. Around this time the Going Merry started to show noticeable signs of damage, such as makeshift wooden repairs to the hull and scraps of steel holding the mast together, leading some members such as Zoro and Sanji to suggest they get a new ship, something Usopp vehemently denies due to its origins.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 210px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b4/Flying_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20131001214718" class="image"><img alt="Flying Merry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="145" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Flying Merry.png" data-image-key="Flying_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b4/Flying_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131001214718" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b4/Flying_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20131001214718" class="image"><img alt="Flying Merry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b4/Flying_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131001214718" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="210" height="145" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Flying Merry.png" data-image-key="Flying_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/b4/Flying_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/210?cb=20131001214718" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Flying_Merry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Going Merry in flying mode.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After several events in Jaya involving <a href="/wiki/Bellamy" title="Bellamy">Bellamy</a> in which the ship was temporarily broken by one of Bellamy's attacks,<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/Saruyama_Alliance" title="Saruyama Alliance">Saruyama Alliance</a> modified her into <b>Going Merry: Flying Mode</b><span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja"></span><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>. A brass brace was attached to the place where Bellamy had rebounded off the ship and split it open, along with four new brass plates on the port and starboard railings to reinforce the Merry. It was also given a rooster motif: wings, a tail, and a decorative red cowl with a cracked eggshell decoration hiding the broken bit of its figurehead. This new design of the Merry was intended so that it could easily maneuver on the vertical current called the <a href="/wiki/Knock_Up_Stream" title="Knock Up Stream">Knock Up Stream</a>. This current was the only way the ship could reach her next destination. Guided by the <a href="/wiki/South_Bird" title="South Bird">South Bird</a> and escorted by <a href="/wiki/Shoujou" title="Shoujou">Shoujou</a> and <a href="/wiki/Masira" title="Masira">Masira</a>'s ships, the Going Merry was taken to the spot where the Knock Up Stream would occur. Once there, the ship was catapulted into the sky by the current. The Going Merry literally flew as it journeyed to the sky. After a momentous journey into the sky, the ship finally landed in the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Clouds#White_Sea" title="Sea Clouds">White Sea</a> where the Straw Hats' adventures in the sky would begin. Unfortunately, the Merry's flying modifications did not hold up for long, as its wings broke off from the force of the landing.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Skypiea_Arc">Skypiea Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D37&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After a brief encounter with a masked warrior and a seemingly errant knight, the Going Merry traveled across the White Sea towards Heaven's Gate. There, the Going Merry was transported to the White-White Sea by the speedy shrimp. Once in the <a href="/wiki/Sea_Clouds#White-White_Sea" title="Sea Clouds">White-White Sea</a>, the Going Merry docked on the shores of <a href="/wiki/Skypiea#Angel_Island" title="Skypiea">Angel Island</a>. Several events caused by the crew happened on Angel Island which ultimately led to the Going Merry to being carried off by a super-express speed lobster deep into <a href="/wiki/Upper_Yard" title="Upper Yard">Upper Yard</a>, the territory of Skypiea's God. This series of events caused the Straw Hats that were left on Angel Island, Luffy, Sanji, and Usopp, to head out into Upper Yard to reclaim their ship and rescue their friends. As for the remaining Straw Hats aboard the Going Merry, they could not do anything to the giant lobster without falling victim to some pursuing sky sharks, so they allowed the lobster to carry the ship until it placed them upon a sacrificial altar surrounded by water-like clouds. There they decided to explore the rest of Upper Yard, leaving Chopper to guard the Going Merry.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While waiting for the others, Chopper encountered one of the priests of Skypiea, <a href="/wiki/Shura" title="Shura">Shura</a> the Sky Rider. Desiring to maintain the balance caused by the other sacrifices (Nami, Zoro, and Robin) leaving the ship, Shura went to the ruined altar of Shandora, where offerings would be taken by the Super-Express Speedy Lobster. He attempted to sacrifice Chopper and began attacking him along with <a href="/wiki/Fuza" title="Fuza">Fuza</a>, and their scuffle began to damage the Merry. The priest, having no respect for the ship, lit the ship's mast on fire. Desperately, Chopper broke the mast and threw it into the clouds in order to prevent the fire from spreading to the rest of the ship. This seemed like a dangerous situation for the Going Merry; however, before the priest could continue his attack on it, her then sole defender, the knight errant, Gan Fall, appeared to fight him off. The battle between these two, however, ended with <a href="/wiki/Gan_Fall" title="Gan Fall">Gan Fall</a> being defeated and Chopper diving into the clouds surrounding the altar to save him, although as a devil fruit user, he lost the ability to swim. Fortunately, the Going Merry wasn't further harassed by the priest as he was then called at that moment to be somewhere else. The Going Merry, then and there, would remain on the altar in its damaged state until the rest of the Straw Hats returned.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20150708001137" class="image"><img alt="Klabautermann Fixing Merry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Klabautermann Fixing Merry.png" data-image-key="Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20150708001137" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20150708001137" class="image"><img alt="Klabautermann Fixing Merry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20150708001137" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="173" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Klabautermann Fixing Merry.png" data-image-key="Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/a/a8/Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20150708001137" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Klabautermann_Fixing_Merry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">A mysterious figure fixes the ship in the middle of the night.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the entire crew rejoined one another and had a party with some wolves, something mysterious happened to the Going Merry. While the rest of the crew was asleep, Usopp went off to relieve himself. As he finishes doing his business, he sees <a href="/wiki/Klabautermann" title="Klabautermann">someone</a> apparently repairing the ship. Wondering who it might be, Usopp tried to get a better look at the person. Suddenly without warning, the person then looked at Usopp with nothing but a smiling featureless face. Horrified by the sight, Usopp wakes the rest of the crew to alert them to what he thinks is a ghost. Seeing no one near the ship, the rest of the crew dismisses Usopp's claims as nothing more than his imagination and go back to sleep. The next morning, however, the crew awaken to a surprising sight. The Going Merry, though still not perfect, was apparently repaired by someone overnight. This was very surprising as most of them knew for sure that no one else was up repairing the ship. What was more surprising was that the one who repaired the ship restored it to its non-flying mode. This was a design that only the crew themselves knew since entering Skypiea. Regardless of who repaired Merry, the crew decided to press forward on their adventure in Skypiea.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After using a sky shark to drag the ship off the altar, it was decided that the Going Merry would be steered to the southern part of Upper Yard. The crew had decided to split up into two teams and that there they would meet up again after getting the gold. However, things did not go as planned when the Merry set off. <a href="/wiki/Enel" title="Enel">Enel</a>, the self-proclaimed God of Skypiea, appeared on the ship and took out Sanji and Usopp. Later the ship was turned into a battleground for Nami and Gan Fall against <a href="/wiki/Satori" title="Satori">Satori</a>'s triplet brothers, <a href="/wiki/Hotori_and_Kotori" title="Hotori and Kotori">Hotori and Kotori</a>. The battle was won by the former. After several events, the ship was left in the protection of <a href="/wiki/Conis" title="Conis">Conis</a> then later her fox, <a href="/wiki/Su" title="Su">Su</a>. Throughout the terror that Enel had brought about with his plan to destroy Skypiea, the ship swayed uneasily against the waves of clouds that were created. It stayed there on that spot for some time, even after the final battle between Enel and Luffy, until the crew returned with bags of gold they supposedly "stole" from Skypiea.
</p><p>After all the excitement in Skypiea, the Going Merry was steered into the direction of <a href="/wiki/Cloud_End" title="Cloud End">Cloud End</a>. There, the Going Merry and her crew left Skypiea, with the aid of a balloon octopus and a hoard of gold. It then safely returned to the <a href="/wiki/Blue_Sea" title="Blue Sea">Blue Sea</a> down below to continue its voyage.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_7_Saga">Water 7 Saga</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D40&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Long_Ring_Long_Land_Arc">Long Ring Long Land Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D41&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>The ship eventually reaches the coast of <a href="/wiki/Long_Ring_Long_Land" title="Long Ring Long Land">Long Ring Long Land</a> where it is docked and then surrounded by the <a href="/wiki/Foxy_Pirates" title="Foxy Pirates">Foxy Pirates</a> and their ship the <a href="/wiki/Sexy_Foxy" title="Sexy Foxy">Sexy Foxy</a>, essentially trapping the Merry in that location until the events of the <a href="/wiki/Davy_Back_Fight" title="Davy Back Fight">Davy Back Fight</a> have concluded.
</p>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="The_Giant_Mechanical_Soldier_of_Karakuri_Castle">The Giant Mechanical Soldier of Karakuri Castle</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D45&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<table style="background: #D8E9FC; color: #000 ; width: 60%; margin: 0em auto 0.8em; padding:0.5em; border-radius:0.4em; -moz-border-radius:0.4em;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="4">

<td><span style="font-size:95%"><b>This is an <a href="/wiki/Category:Pages_With_Empty_Sections" title="Category:Pages With Empty Sections"><font color="maroon">empty section</font></a>. Please help the wiki by adding information to it.</b><span>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Water_7_Arc">Water 7 Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D46&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>After the ship returned to the Blue Sea and the events the crew experienced in <a href="/wiki/Long_Ring_Long_Land" title="Long Ring Long Land">Long Ring Long Land</a> also ended, the Going Merry's crew had reached the fabled city of water, <a href="/wiki/Water_7" title="Water 7">Water 7</a>. This Venice-like city was renowned for its shipwrights and shipyards. So great were these, that not even pirates dared to attack them at risk of not having their ships repaired or worse. This city was a great opportunity for the Straw Hats in many ways. Ever since the damage caused by the marines during the Straw Hat's escape from Arabasta, the Going Merry had continued to sustain heavy damage caused by a number of events. Even though the crew, most notably Usopp, was able to patch up the Merry, the repairs done to the ship were below standard. Here, the Straw Hats could finally fully repair the ship properly. Even better, they also hoped to gain a new member for the crew from the abundance of <a href="/wiki/Shipwright" title="Shipwright">shipwrights</a> within the city. This they hoped would help maintain the ship fully. With these high hopes, they docked the Going Merry on a shore near the city.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/61/Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20230520172920" class="image"><img alt="Kaku Evaluating the Merry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Kaku Evaluating the Merry.png" data-image-key="Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/61/Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230520172920" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/61/Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20230520172920" class="image"><img alt="Kaku Evaluating the Merry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/61/Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230520172920" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Kaku Evaluating the Merry.png" data-image-key="Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/6/61/Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230520172920" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Kaku_Evaluating_the_Merry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Kaku evaluates the Going Merry's condition.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After renting some Yagara Bulls and exchanging the gold they acquired from Skypiea for a total of <span style="white-space:nowrap;"><a href="/wiki/Belly" title="Belly"><img alt="Beli" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="12" height="20" data-image-name="Beli.png" data-image-key="Beli.png" data-relevant="0" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/d/de/Beli.png/revision/latest?cb=20141206091723" class="lazyload" /></a></span>300,000,000, Luffy, Nami, and Usopp proceeded to Dock One where they met <a href="/wiki/Kaku" title="Kaku">Kaku</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> and then later President <a href="/wiki/Iceburg" title="Iceburg">Iceburg</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Galley-La_Company" title="Galley-La Company">Galley-La Company</a> and two other foremen working there. Seeing as they were customers then, Kaku decided to check out their ship. Unfortunately, upon returning, the shipwright brought bad news. The Going Merry was now irreparable.
</p><p>This, as Kaku explained, was because the keel (which is like a ship's backbone) was broken. This was the most critical part of the Going Merry, and it being broken meant the ship could never be fixed again. This meant the ship would practically sink on the way to the next island. Luffy, not wanting to accept this, insisted that the shipwrights repair the ship regardless of the cost. It was then, however, that Luffy and Nami realized that Usopp was missing, along with two-thirds of their money intended to repair the ship. This was done by the <a href="/wiki/Franky_Family" title="Franky Family">Franky Family</a>, a gang of bounty hunters that earlier had attempted to raid the Merry with Zoro on it.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After discovering that Usopp had been taken and beaten up by the Franky Family for the money, Luffy, along with Zoro, Sanji, and Chopper, decided to raid the gang's hideout to reclaim the money, as well avenge their fallen comrade. However, when they trashed the place, they discovered that the money that could have been used to repair the ship had been taken far away from Water 7. With this turn of events and the facts given by the Galley-La company, Luffy made the hard decision to instead buy a new ship. This decision, however, did not go over well with Usopp. Having repaired the ship so many times, Usopp had come to treasure the ship to a point where he considered her as part of the crew. Thus, he could not accept as it seemed to him like the crew was abandoning one of their own. This disagreement with Luffy's decision eventually led to Usopp leaving the crew and a battle between him and Luffy for ownership of the Going Merry. This battle in the night was an intense one for both combatants. This was because Usopp had known Luffy more than the latter's previous opponents and was able to come up with some strategies to battle Luffy for the ship. However, despite all the effort Usopp put into it, Luffy beats him. Even though he was the victor, Luffy let Usopp keep the ship. The next morning, Luffy and the rest of the crew take their belongings off the ship, leaving Usopp alone with the Going Merry.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Klabautermann_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20241022013759" class="image"><img alt="Klabautermann Infobox" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="207" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Klabautermann Infobox.png" data-image-key="Klabautermann_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Klabautermann_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20241022013759" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Klabautermann_Infobox.png/revision/latest?cb=20241022013759" class="image"><img alt="Klabautermann Infobox" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Klabautermann_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20241022013759" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="207" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Klabautermann Infobox.png" data-image-key="Klabautermann_Infobox.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/5/56/Klabautermann_Infobox.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20241022013759" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Klabautermann_Infobox.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Klabautermann as described by Franky.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the intense battle from the night before, Usopp continued to desperately repair the Going Merry, despite his lack of carpentry skills and equipment. Eventually, Usopp is "kidnapped" by the boss of the Franky Family, <a href="/wiki/Franky" title="Franky">Franky</a>, in order to draw out Luffy whom the latter had a brief battle with. Usopp and the ship are then taken to Franky's secret hideout under the bridge. Despite being enemies, the two bonded together and Franky allowed Usopp to continue repairing the ship. However, after hearing Usopp plans to use the Going Merry to go back home, Franky began to dismantle the ship despite Usopp's protests. The underworld boss told Usopp the same reason Kaku told him as to why the ship could not be repaired anymore. Usopp, knowing this all too well, replied that he knew already that the ship could no longer be repaired but did not have the heart to accept it. It is then that Usopp revealed to Franky about the mysterious spirit that he saw. Realizing what Usopp was talking about, Franky explained to Usopp that the spirit he saw was a <a href="/wiki/Klabautermann" title="Klabautermann">Klabautermann</a>, a manifestation of a ship's soul brought about when it has been loved and cared enough. Franky explained to Usopp that the Going Merry is a ship whose final job now is to carry its crew to one last island before it could sink. Should she not be able to do so, the ship would have failed in her duty. She, he explained, would be happier to simply be dismantled at an island than to sink with her crew onboard. This explanation made Usopp realize how much more of a crewmate the ship was. However, it also led to a heated debate between him and Franky on whether or not the ship should be dismantled. Before the debate could get any more heated, Franky's hideout was breached. The intruders who barged in were Lucci, Kaku, Kalifa, and Blueno, four of the shipwrights of Water 7 who were then revealed to be secret undercover agents of <a href="/wiki/CP9" title="CP9">Cipher Pol 9</a>.
</p><p>After a brief struggle wherein, the agents took down Franky in order to get the blueprints of the ancient weapon, <a href="/wiki/Pluton" title="Pluton">Pluton</a>, the Going Merry was put in a dire situation. One of the agents, Kaku, explained that even though the agents were undercover and not truly shipwrights by trade, they had studied up on the job rigorously in order to function as shipwrights well enough to avert suspicion. The group's judgment that the ship needed to be scuttled was a legitimate call by professionals who had the knowledge needed to make it. As one last act as a shipwright, Kaku cast off the Going Merry out into the sea where the fury of the <a href="/wiki/Aqua_Laguna" title="Aqua Laguna">Aqua Laguna</a> was currently besieging Water 7. With a mighty fall from the hideout, the Going Merry plunged into the raging sea.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Enies_Lobby_Arc">Enies Lobby Arc</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D47&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 220px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117011439" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry Saves The Crew" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry Saves The Crew.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230117011439" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png/revision/latest?cb=20230117011439" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry Saves The Crew" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230117011439" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="220" height="124" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry Saves The Crew.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/7/73/Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/220?cb=20230117011439" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry_Saves_The_Crew.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">The Going Merry saving everyone in Enies Lobby.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>After the discovery of CP9 and its intentions, the Straw Hats and their allies leave Water 7 and are drawn to the judiciary island, <a href="/wiki/Enies_Lobby" title="Enies Lobby">Enies Lobby</a>, to battle against the World Government and the numerous forces stationed there. This invasion ultimately leads to a massive battle on the Bridge of Hesitation between the pirates and a horde of Marines deployed by the Buster Call ships.
</p><p>The battle was very intense due to the fact that most of the Marines weren't the run of the mill kind plus there was also the impending danger of the Buster Call cannons. Just when it all seemed hopeless, the Going Merry suddenly appeared out of nowhere.
</p>
<table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" style="width:100%; clear:both;">
</table><table class="noprint" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" border="0" align="center" style="background:none; text-align:center;">
 <tbody><tr>
  <td style="vertical-align:top; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding:.3em 0em 0em 0em; text-shadow: 1px -1px gray;">“</td>
  <td style="padding:1em 1em; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif;; font-style:italic; font-size:medium; color:inherit;">Let's go everyone...!!<br />Back to the sea of adventure again!!<br />I came to take you home!!
</td>
  <td style="vertical-align:bottom; font-size:3em; color:#88B7FD; font-family:&#39;Times New Roman&#39;,serif; font-weight:bold; padding-bottom:0em; padding-left:0em; padding-right:0em; text-shadow: -1px 1px gray;">”</td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>
<table style="padding-right: 2%; font-size:80%; text-align:right; width:100%;">
 <tbody><tr valign="top">
  <td><cite style="font-family:&#39;Arial&#39;,sans-serif;">—&#160;Merry coming to pick up its comrades.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup></cite>
  </td>
 </tr>
</tbody></table>

<p><br />
Without hesitation, the Straw Hats and their allies boarded the ship and made a desperate escape. With a little thrust from Franky's Coup de Vent and a little gate closing thanks to Sanji, the Going Merry and her crew escaped from Enies Lobby leaving the Buster Call ships to deal with the whirlpools. With this, the battle in Enies Lobby was won.
</p><p>Having escaped Enies Lobby on the Going Merry, everything seemed right in the world for the Straw Hats. Unfortunately, the joy was short lived. The Going Merry suddenly broke apart in the middle of the ocean. Fortunately, a Galley-La ship carrying Iceburg and other workers appeared to rescue the passengers on board the Going Merry in time. Upon reuniting with the president since they left Water 7, Iceburg revealed the Going Merry's sudden appearance at Enies Lobby. After they had left Water 7 for Enies Lobby, Iceburg found the ship beached on one of Water 7's shores, surprisingly undamaged from the fall. The ship then apparently asked Iceburg to fix her. Iceburg, though shocked at hearing the voice and found the damage to be irreparable, reluctantly complied, using his expertise to patch up the ship enough for it to sail for a limited time. To his surprise once again, the ship thanked him and then suddenly set off by itself into the raging seas, braving the <a href="/wiki/Aqua_Laguna" title="Aqua Laguna">storm</a> that was then going on. He also told them that the ship was now in a state completely beyond repair and needed to finally rest in peace and that she was a special ship, treated with care.
</p>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20230510014253" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Funeral" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="129" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230510014253" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest?cb=20230510014253" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry&#39;s Funeral" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230510014253" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="129" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry&#39;s Funeral.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/1/1d/Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20230510014253" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry%27s_Funeral.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Going Merry's funeral.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>With heavy hearts, Luffy set the ship on fire and the Going Merry was given a Viking funeral; Luffy, unaware of <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Sogeking</a>'s identity, thought it would be better if Usopp was not here for this, fearing he would be unable to take it. The Straw Hats stayed to see Merry off, not wanting it to leave lonely. As the ship was burned, snow appeared and the Merry spoke to her crew. Despite the crew feeling like they really did not take care of the ship to the fullest during her time with them, the Going Merry did not hold any hard feelings towards them. This, as she explained, was because the crew actually did take care of her, and for that, she was grateful. As Merry apologized to the crew that it wanted to take them "a little further", Luffy cried back that they are the ones who should be apologizing for their way of treating the ship; Merry assured them it was happy. With her last words and a tearful goodbye from her crew, the Going Merry was finally destroyed, and an invaluable member was forever lost.<sup id="cite_ref-c430_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c430-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Legacy">Legacy</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D48&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>On board the <a href="/wiki/Thousand_Sunny" title="Thousand Sunny">Thousand Sunny</a>, Franky announced that the Thousand Sunny will carry on the spirit of Going Merry. This is shown more literally when Franky later introduced the Straw Hat Pirates to the soldier dock system and it was revealed that Channel 2 houses the <a href="/wiki/Mini_Merry_II" title="Mini Merry II">Mini Merry II</a>, a four-passenger steamboat almost identical to the original Merry, so much that Usopp declared that she was Merry's "reincarnation"; the main differences are that it is much smaller and has a steam engine with paddle wheels.
</p><p>Usopp, who was so dedicated to saving Merry that it blinded him from the truth to the point of nearly severing his ties with the rest of the Straw Hat Pirates, came to realize his mistake upon Merry's funeral. Although difficult, he accepted that he had to let the ship go, and eventually went to apologize to the crew before being re-accepted.
</p><p><small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>The following events are <a href="/wiki/Canon#Non-Canon" title="Canon">Non-Canon</a> and therefore not considered part of the <a href="/wiki/Canon" title="Canon">Canon</a> story.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<p>When Usopp, Chopper and <a href="/wiki/Brook" title="Brook">Brook</a> were riding on the Mini Merry II, Brook asked about the little ship's design. Remembering that Brook was recruited after the Going Merry's demise, Usopp <a href="/wiki/Episode_of_Merry" title="Episode of Merry">recounted</a> to him about how the Merry was their first ship and all the adventures they had together. Touched by the Going Merry's life story, Brook cried that he would have wanted to meet the ship. When back aboard the Thousand Sunny, Usopp caught a glimpse of Merry's <a href="/wiki/Klabautermann" title="Klabautermann">Klabautermann</a> and shed a tear for the ship that he loved so much.
<small>
</small></p><small><hr /></small><small><p><span style="color:red;"><i><b>Concludes non-canon section.</b></i></span>
</p></small><small><hr /></small>
<p>The ship of the <a href="/wiki/Barto_Club" title="Barto Club">Barto Club</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Going_Luffy-senpai" title="Going Luffy-senpai">Going Luffy-senpai</a> is clearly a homage to Merry, possessing a similar name and design.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Adaptation_Differences">Adaptation Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D49&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Anime_Differences">Anime Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D50&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 150px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest?cb=20100817234446" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry Color Scheme" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="254" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Going Merry Color Scheme.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100817234446" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest?cb=20100817234446" class="image"><img alt="Going Merry Color Scheme" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100817234446" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="150" height="254" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Going Merry Color Scheme.png" data-image-key="Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/b/bd/Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/150?cb=20100817234446" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Going_Merry_Color_Scheme.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Going Merry as commonly colored in the manga.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>While the manga (in both <a href="/wiki/Chapters_and_Volumes" title="Chapters and Volumes">volume</a> covers and <a href="/wiki/Cover_Page" title="Cover Page">color spreads</a>) consistently depicted the Going Merry with a conservative brown color-scheme, the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Anime)" title="One Piece (Anime)">anime</a> gave a solid white color to much of its trim and—most prominently—the sheep figurehead. The latter design has been followed by most if not all of the series' merchandise and promotional materials (except the <a href="/wiki/Digitally_Colored_Manga" title="Digitally Colored Manga">Digitally Colored Manga</a>, which follows the original).
</p><p>In the manga, the Going Merry had been accumulating damage on her voyage in the Grand Line, with the most notable damage happening with the Straw Hat pirates encounter with <a href="/wiki/Laboon" title="Laboon">Laboon</a> (the figurehead breaks and Luffy tears off one of the masts to use as a weapon), <a href="/wiki/Wapol" title="Wapol">Wapol</a> (an entire part of the ship's side gets <a href="/wiki/Baku_Baku_no_Mi" title="Baku Baku no Mi">eaten</a> by him) and later taking heavier damage while escaping from the Marines during the Straw Hat's departure from <a href="/wiki/Arabasta_Kingdom" title="Arabasta Kingdom">Arabasta</a> (several massive iron harpoons pierce the ship). In the anime, this damage is more or less removed unexpectedly,<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> and they sustain most of it from their <a href="/wiki/Ruluka_Island_Arc" title="Ruluka Island Arc">adventures in the Rainbow Mist</a> when the ship is catapulted out of <a href="/wiki/Rainbow_Mist" title="Rainbow Mist">Ape's concert</a>, tearing apart from the shockwaves it endures.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Live-Action_Differences">Live-Action Differences</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D51&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_(Live-Action_Series)" title="One Piece (Live-Action Series)">live-action series</a>, because Merry is killed by Kuro unlike in the manga,<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> the <i>Going Merry</i> is named by Luffy in honor of Merry.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> The figurehead of the ship is also of a more realistic sheepshead.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Real-life_Counterpart">Real-life Counterpart</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D52&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tleft show-info-icon" style="width: 230px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Real_Going_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20130124171946" class="image"><img alt="Real Going Merry" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="153" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Real Going Merry.png" data-image-key="Real_Going_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Real_Going_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130124171946" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Real_Going_Merry.png/revision/latest?cb=20130124171946" class="image"><img alt="Real Going Merry" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Real_Going_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130124171946" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="230" height="153" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Real Going Merry.png" data-image-key="Real_Going_Merry.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/4/42/Real_Going_Merry.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/230?cb=20130124171946" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Real_Going_Merry.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption"><i>Real Life Going Merry</i>.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<p>In 2003, a replica of the <i>Going Merry</i>, which may not be fully functional, was created and has been present at a number of exhibitions sponsored by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shueisha" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Shueisha">Shueisha</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toei_Animation" title="Toei Animation">Toei Animation</a>, and <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fuji_TV" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Fuji TV">Fuji TV</a>, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Odaiba" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Odaiba">Odaiba</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tokyo" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Tokyo">Tokyo</a>. The 2005 incarnation of this live-action replica is designed to show the beating the ship had taken up through the <a href="/wiki/Water_7_Arc" title="Water 7 Arc">Water 7 Arc</a>.<br style="clear:both;" />
</p><p><br />
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Translation_and_Dub_Issues">Translation and Dub Issues</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D53&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the <a href="/wiki/Odex" title="Odex">Odex</a> version of the anime, when the Straw Hats first receive the Going Merry in <a href="/wiki/Episode_17" title="Episode 17">Episode 17</a>, Merry neglects to say its name and it is exclusively referred to as "the ship" and "the boat". This continues for several episodes, until <a href="/wiki/Episode_31" title="Episode 31">Episode 31</a> when Usopp spots the stolen ship and finally refers to it as <i>the Going Merry</i>.
</p><p>Also in the Odex dub, when introducing the ship, instead of saying he designed the ship, Merry states that he renovated and restored it. Merry also says that the ship is a "caravan" rather than a caravel ("caravan" is not actually a type of ship) and that it is "from the 15th century, used mainly by the Spanish and Portuguese on their voyage." He does not specify what voyage he's referring to but it can be inferred he's referring to the various transatlantic voyages made during the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Age_of_Discovery" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Age of Discovery">Age of Discovery</a>. He also states that "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Christopher_Columbus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Christopher Columbus">Christopher Columbus</a> commanded this type of ship when he discovered America." This would actually be correct if he had said it was a caravel rather than "caravan". Obviously America, Spain, Portugal and Christopher Columbus are never stated to exist within the original canon.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Merchandise">Merchandise</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D54&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Going Merry figurines are presented in several merchandise series, including <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Wobbling_Pirate_Ship_Collection" title="One Piece Wobbling Pirate Ship Collection">One Piece Wobbling Pirate Ship Collection</a> and <a href="/wiki/One_Piece_Super_Ship_Collection" title="One Piece Super Ship Collection">One Piece Super Ship Collection</a>.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Cultural_References">Cultural References</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D55&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>In the <a href="https://disney.fandom.com/wiki/Coney_Island,_Baby!" class="extiw" title="w:c:disney:Coney Island, Baby!">fourteenth episode</a> of <i><a href="https://disney.fandom.com/wiki/Moon_Girl_and_Devil_Dinosaur" class="extiw" title="w:c:disney:Moon Girl and Devil Dinosaur">Moon Girl and Devil Dinosaur</a></i>, a merry-go-round is depicted with the name Going Merrily and a logo showing the mast of the Going Merry.
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Trivia">Trivia</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a title="Sign in to edit" class="mw-editsection-visualeditor" data-tracking-label="log-in-edit-section" data-action="edit-section" href="https://auth.fandom.com/signin?redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fonepiece.fandom.com%2Fwiki%2FGoing_Merry%3Fveaction%3Dedit%26section%3D56&amp;uselang=en" data-testid="log-in-edit-section"><svg class="wds-icon wds-icon-tiny"><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-pencil-tiny"></use></svg></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<figure class="thumb tright show-info-icon" style="width: 120px"> 	<a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png/revision/latest?cb=20190301100751" class="image"><img alt="Merry&#39;s Personal Jolly Roger" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIABAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAEALAAAAAABAAEAQAICTAEAOw%3D%3D" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="107" class="thumbimage lazyload" data-image-name="Merry&#39;s Personal Jolly Roger.png" data-image-key="Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20190301100751" /></a> 	<noscript><a href="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png/revision/latest?cb=20190301100751" class="image"><img alt="Merry&#39;s Personal Jolly Roger" src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20190301100751" decoding="async" loading="lazy" width="120" height="107" class="thumbimage" data-image-name="Merry&#39;s Personal Jolly Roger.png" data-image-key="Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png" data-relevant="1" data-src="https://static.wikia.nocookie.net/onepiece/images/e/e8/Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png/revision/latest/scale-to-width-down/120?cb=20190301100751" /></a></noscript> 	<figcaption class="thumbcaption"> 		 			<a href="/wiki/File:Merry%27s_Personal_Jolly_Roger.png" class="info-icon"><svg><use xlink:href="#wds-icons-info-small"></use></svg></a> 		 		 		 			<p class="caption">Merry's personal Jolly Roger on the main mast.</p> 		 	</figcaption> </figure>
<ul><li>Until <a href="/wiki/Usopp" title="Usopp">Usopp</a> drew the crew's <a href="/wiki/Jolly_Roger" title="Jolly Roger">Jolly Roger</a>, the ship sailed under <a href="/wiki/Merry" title="Merry">Merry</a>'s personal Jolly Roger.</li>
<li>Caravel class ships were one of the few ships designed for sea travel that also could travel inland via rivers. Due to their lightness, caravels were faster and more agile than many of the bigger ships. As such, merchants favored them highly despite their low cargo hold. Yet despite their advantages, as the Going Merry implied, they were fragile vessels that could not take as much battering as many other vessels could.</li>
<li>The Going Merry was voiced by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Houko_Kuwashima" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Houko Kuwashima">Houko Kuwashima</a>, and in the English dub, by <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Brittney_Karbowski" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Brittney Karbowski">Brittney Karbowski</a>.</li>
<li>The Going Merry referred itself as "Boku"<span style="font-weight: normal"> (<span class="t_nihongo_kanji" lang="ja">僕</span><span class="t_nihongo_comma">,</span> <i><span class="t_nihongo_romaji">Boku</span></i><span class="t_nihongo_help"><sup><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Help:Japanese" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Help:Japanese"><span class="t_nihongo_icon" style="color:#00e;font:bold 80% sans-serif;text-decoration:none;padding:0 .1em;">?</span></a></sup></span>)</span>, a masculine pronoun used by males, usually meant to be humble and for boys (or young men).<sup id="cite_ref-c430_5-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-c430-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>Despite its initial color scheme and design, on the <a href="/wiki/Cover_Page" title="Cover Page">Cover Page</a> of <a href="/wiki/Chapter_967" title="Chapter 967">Chapter 967</a>, the ship was seen with a white figure head.</li>
<li>The Going Merry is one of the very few ships in the series shown to be destroyed via deliberate scuttling.</li></ul>
